> Project Part: Smart Plating (10/min)
  # Alternate: Plastic Smart Plating:
    | Input/Output and Step Efficiency Values:
        - 5 Reinforced Iron Plate(s)
        - 5 Rotor(s)
        - 15 Plastic(s)
        - 55 MW(s)
        * 1 Manufacturer(s)
        * 342 m^2(s) (about 6 foundations minus belt space)
        * 2 steps into the chain from the top.
        ++ 10 Project Part: Smart Plating per minute
